from rest_framework.response import Response

from api.common.decorators import log_api_call
from api.common.mixins import BaseAPIView
from api.common.routers import CustomViewRouter
from api.partners.auth.permissions import HasDashboardAccess
from api.partners.common.services import PartnerIoTService
from api.partners.vendor.serializers import IoTHistorySerializer

partner_iot_router = CustomViewRouter()


@partner_iot_router.register(r"partner/iot/history", name="partner-iot-history")
@extend_schema(
    tags=["Partner - IoT"],
    summary="Get IoT History",
    description="Get partner IoT action history",
    responses={200: IoTHistorySerializer(many=True)}
)
class PartnerIoTHistoryView(GenericAPIView, BaseAPIView):
    """IoT action history for partners"""
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated, HasDashboardAccess]

    @log_api_call()
    def get(self, request: Request) -> Response:
        """Get IoT action history"""
        def operation():
            partner = request.user.partner
            service = PartnerIoTService()

            filters = {
                'action_type': request.query_params.get('action_type'),
                'start_date': request.query_params.get('start_date'),
                'end_date': request.query_params.get('end_date'),
                'page': int(request.query_params.get('page', 1)),
                'page_size': int(request.query_params.get('page_size', 20))
            }

            result = service.get_iot_history(partner, filters)
            serializer = IoTHistorySerializer(result['results'], many=True)

            return {
                'count': result['count'],
                'next': result['next'],
                'previous': result['previous'],
                'results': serializer.data
            }

        return self.handle_service_operation(
            operation,
            "IoT history retrieved successfully",
            "Failed to retrieve IoT history"
        )
'''

+    162: # Service: FranchisePayoutService
+    163: def get_vendor_payouts(self, franchise, filters):
+    164:     # Get payouts from franchise's vendors
+    165:     vendor_ids = PartnerRepository.get_child_partners(
+    166:         str(franchise.id)
+    167:     ).values_list('id', flat=True)
+    168:
+    169:     filters['partner_id__in'] = vendor_ids
+    170:     filters['payout_type'] = 'FRANCHISE_TO_VENDOR'
+    171:
+    172:     return PayoutRequestRepository.filter_payouts(filters)
+    173:
+    174: def approve_vendor_payout(self, franchise, payout_id):
+    175:     payout = self._validate_vendor_payout(franchise, payout_id)
+    176:
+    177:     if payout.status != 'PENDING':
+    178:         raise ServiceException("Can only approve PENDING payouts")
+    179:
+    180:     return PayoutRequestRepository.update(
+    181:         payout_id,
+    182:         status='APPROVED',
+    183:         approved_at=timezone.now()
+    184:     )
+    185:
+    186: def complete_vendor_payout(self, franchise, payout_id):
+    187:     payout = self._validate_vendor_payout(franchise, payout_id)
+    188:
+    189:     if payout.status != 'APPROVED':
+    190:         raise ServiceException("Can only complete APPROVED payouts")
+    191:
+    192:     # Deduct from franchise balance
+    193:     PartnerRepository.update_balance(
+    194:         str(franchise.id),
+    195:         payout.amount,
+    196:         add=False
+    197:     )
+    198:
+    199:     # Deduct from vendor balance
+    200:     PartnerRepository.update_balance(
+    201:         str(payout.partner_id),
+    202:         payout.amount,
+    203:         add=False
+    204:     )
+    205:
+    206:     return PayoutRequestRepository.update(
+    207:         payout_id,
+    208:         status='COMPLETED',
+    209:         completed_at=timezone.now()
+    210:     )
+    211:
+    212: def reject_vendor_payout(self, franchise, payout_id, reason):
+    213:     payout = self._validate_vendor_payout(franchise, payout_id)
+    214:
+    215:     if payout.status not in ['PENDING', 'APPROVED']:
+    216:         raise ServiceException("Cannot reject completed payout")
+    217:
+    218:     return PayoutRequestRepository.update(
+    219:         payout_id,
+    220:         status='REJECTED',
+    221:         rejection_reason=reason
+    222:     )
+    223:
+    224: def _validate_vendor_payout(self, franchise, payout_id):
+    225:     payout = PayoutRequestRepository.get_by_id(payout_id)
+    226:     if not payout:
+    227:         raise ServiceException("Payout not found")
+    228:
+    229:     # Check if vendor belongs to franchise
+    230:     vendor = PartnerRepository.get_by_id(str(payout.partner_id))
+    231:     if vendor.parent_id != franchise.id:
+    232:         raise ServiceException("Not your vendor's payout")
+    233:
+    234:     return payout
+    235: ```

+    294:

+    296:         return None
+    297:

+    299:         str(distribution.id)
+    300:     )
+    301:
+    302:     if not revenue_share:
+    303:         return None
+    304:
+    305:     return {
+    306:         'station_id': str(distribution.station_id),
+    307:         'station_name': distribution.station.name,

+    309:         'partner_percent': revenue_share.partner_percent,

   - Used by rental cancellation system

### 3. Views Pattern Correction
Fixed all views to follow exact user pattern:
```python
@router.register(r"path", name="name")
@extend_schema(                          # OUTSIDE class
    tags=["Partner - Franchise"],
    summary="Summary",
    responses={200: Serializer}
)
class ViewName(GenericAPIView, BaseAPIView):
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated, HasDashboardAccess]
    serializer_class = RequestSerializer  # For POST/PATCH

    @log_api_call()                      # NO extend_schema here
    def get(self, request):
        ...
```

### Key Business Rules Implemented
- BR2.3: Vendor can have ONLY ONE station (StationAssignmentService)
- BR3.1: One station = one active distribution (StationAssignmentService)
- BR3.3: Revenue model - Fixed OR Percentage (StationAssignmentService)
- BR3.4: Non-Revenue vendors have NO revenue model (StationAssignmentService)
- BR6: Payout flow (PENDING → APPROVED → PROCESSING → COMPLETED)
- BR12: Visibility (franchise sees own+vendors, vendor sees only own)
- BR13.2: Free ejection (1/day per vendor via PartnerIoTService)

### Permission Classes Used
From api/partners/auth/permissions.py:
- IsAuthenticated (DRF standard)
- HasDashboardAccess (Franchise OR Revenue Vendor)
- IsActivePartner (base class)
- IsFranchise, IsRevenueVendor (specific types)

from rest_framework.generics import GenericAPIView
from rest_framework.response import Response
from rest_framework import status

from api.common.views import BaseAPIView
from api.common.decorators import log_api_call
from api.partners.auth.permissions import IsAuthenticated, HasDashboardAccess

    VendorUpdateSerializer,

from api.web.routers import CustomRouter

router = CustomRouter()


@router.register(r"vendors", name="franchise-vendors")
@extend_schema(
    tags=["Partner - Franchise"],
    summary="Franchise vendor management",
    description="List, create, update, and delete vendors under franchise"
)
class FranchiseVendorView(GenericAPIView, BaseAPIView):
    """Franchise vendor management view"""
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated, HasDashboardAccess]
    serializer_class = VendorCreateSerializer

    def __init__(self, **kwargs):
        super().__init__(**kwargs)
        self.vendor_service = FranchiseVendorService()

    @extend_schema(
        responses={200: VendorListSerializer(many=True)},
        parameters=[
            OpenApiParameter('status', str, description='Filter by status'),
            OpenApiParameter('search', str, description='Search by name/code'),
        ]
    )
    @log_api_call()
    def get(self, request):
        """List all vendors under franchise"""
        franchise = request.user.partner

        filters = {}
        if request.query_params.get('status'):
            filters['status'] = request.query_params['status']
        if request.query_params.get('search'):
            filters['search'] = request.query_params['search']

        vendors = self.vendor_service.list_vendors(franchise, **filters)
        serializer = VendorListSerializer(vendors, many=True)

        return Response(serializer.data)

    @extend_schema(
        request=VendorCreateSerializer,
        responses={201: VendorDetailSerializer}
    )
    @log_api_call()
    def post(self, request):
        """Create new vendor"""
        franchise = request.user.partner

        serializer = VendorCreateSerializer(data=request.data)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)

        vendor = self.vendor_service.create_vendor(
            franchise,
            serializer.validated_data
        )

        response_serializer = VendorDetailSerializer(vendor)
        return Response(
            response_serializer.data,
            status=status.HTTP_201_CREATED
        )


@router.register(r"vendors/{id}", name="franchise-vendor-detail")
@extend_schema(
    tags=["Partner - Franchise"],
    summary="Franchise vendor detail operations",
    description="Get, update, or delete specific vendor"
)
class FranchiseVendorDetailView(GenericAPIView, BaseAPIView):
    """Franchise vendor detail view"""
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated, HasDashboardAccess]
    serializer_class = VendorUpdateSerializer

    def __init__(self, **kwargs):
        super().__init__(**kwargs)
        self.vendor_service = FranchiseVendorService()

    @extend_schema(responses={200: VendorDetailSerializer})
    @log_api_call()
    def get(self, request, id):
        """Get vendor details"""
        franchise = request.user.partner
        vendor_data = self.vendor_service.get_vendor_detail(franchise, id)
        serializer = VendorDetailSerializer(vendor_data)
        return Response(serializer.data)

    @extend_schema(
        request=VendorUpdateSerializer,
        responses={200: VendorDetailSerializer}
    )
    @log_api_call()
    def patch(self, request, id):
        """Update vendor"""
        franchise = request.user.partner

        serializer = VendorUpdateSerializer(data=request.data, partial=True)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)

        vendor = self.vendor_service.update_vendor(
            franchise,
            id,
            serializer.validated_data
        )

        response_serializer = VendorDetailSerializer(vendor)
        return Response(response_serializer.data)

    @extend_schema(responses={204: None})
    @log_api_call()
    def delete(self, request, id):
        """Delete vendor"""
        franchise = request.user.partner
        self.vendor_service.delete_vendor(franchise, id)
        return Response(status=status.HTTP_204_NO_CONTENT)

+      144:         """
+      145:         List payout requests from vendors under franchise.
+      146:
+      147:         Args:

+      151:         Returns:
+      152:             Dict with count, next, previous, results
+      153:         """
+      154:         # Get own vendors
+      155:         vendors = PartnerRepository.get_child_partners(str(franchise.id))
+      156:         vendor_ids = [str(v.id) for v in vendors]
+      157:
+      158:         if not vendor_ids:
+      159:             return {
+      160:                 'count': 0,
+      161:                 'next': None,
+      162:                 'previous': None,

+      164:             }

+      197:         Approve vendor payout request.

+      199:         Args:

+      202:
+      203:         Returns:
+      204:             Updated PayoutRequest object
+      205:
+      206:         Raises:
+      207:             ServiceException: If validation fails

+      213:         # Verify vendor belongs to franchise
+      214:         vendor = PartnerRepository.get_by_id(str(payout.partner_id))

+      216:             self.raise_error("Payout request not found or not under your franchise")
+      217:
+      218:         # Verify status

+      220:             self.raise_error(f"Cannot approve payout in {payout.status} status")

+      227:         )

+      233:         Mark vendor payout as completed.

+      238:             data: Dict with transaction_id (optional)

+      240:         Returns:
+      241:             Updated PayoutRequest object
+      242:
+      243:         Raises:
+      244:             ServiceException: If validation fails
+      245:         """

+      248:             self.raise_error("Payout request not found")

+      250:         # Verify vendor belongs to franchise
+      251:         vendor = PartnerRepository.get_by_id(str(payout.partner_id))
+      252:         if not vendor or str(vendor.parent_franchise_id) != str(franchise.id):
+      253:             self.raise_error("Payout request not found or not under your franchise")
+      254:
+      255:         # Verify status

    "email": "franchise@test.com",
    "password": "Test@1234",
    "phone_number": "+9779800000001",

  exit 1

    \"business_name\": \"Test Franchise Ltd\",
    \"contact_phone\": \"+9779800000001\",
    \"contact_email\": \"franchise@test.com\",
    \"address\": \"Kathmandu, Nepal\"
  }")

if [ -z "$FRANCHISE_ID" ]; then
  echo "❌ Failed to create franchise"
  exit 1

echo "✅ Franchise created with ID: $FRANCHISE_ID"

echo "=========================================="

FRANCHISE_LOGIN=$(curl -s -X POST "${BASE_URL}/api/partners/auth/login" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{
    "email": "franchise@test.com",
    "password": "Test@1234"
  }')

  exit 1

from rest_framework import serializers


class VendorAgreementSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    """Serializer for vendor in agreement"""
    id = serializers.UUIDField()
    code = serializers.CharField()
    business_name = serializers.CharField()
    vendor_type = serializers.CharField()
    status = serializers.CharField()


class DistributionAgreementSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    """Serializer for distribution in agreement"""
    id = serializers.UUIDField()
    franchise_id = serializers.UUIDField()
    station_id = serializers.UUIDField()
    vendor_id = serializers.UUIDField(allow_null=True)
    status = serializers.CharField()
    assigned_at = serializers.DateTimeField()


class RevenueShareAgreementSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    """Serializer for revenue share in agreement"""
    id = serializers.UUIDField()
    revenue_model = serializers.CharField()
    partner_percent = serializers.DecimalField(max_digits=5, decimal_places=2, allow_null=True)
    fixed_amount = serializers.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2, allow_null=True)


class AgreementSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    """Serializer for complete agreement"""
    vendor = VendorAgreementSerializer()
    distribution = DistributionAgreementSerializer()
    revenue_share = RevenueShareAgreementSerializer(allow_null=True)


class AgreementListSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    """Serializer for agreement list response"""
    agreements = AgreementSerializer(many=True)
